ENVIRONMENT, CLIMATE CHANGE FOREST 
DEPARTMENT
Declaration of Cherumulli Forest Block-2, Gudalur Taluk, 
The Nilgiris District as Reserved Forest under the 
Tamil Nadu Forest Act.
[G.O. Ms. 53, Environment, Climate Change Forest (FR.14), 
23rd August 2021, ÝõE 7, Hôõ,
F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2052.]
No.II(2)/ECCF/110/2022.— In exercise of the powers 
conferred by section 16-A of the Tamil Nadu Forest Act, 1882 
(Tamil Nadu Act V of 1882), the Governor of Tamil Nadu 
hereby declares the land vested with the  Government Under 
the Gudalur Janmam Estates (Abolition and Conversion into 
Ryotwari Act, 1969  (Tamil Nadu Act 24 of 1969) and already 
determined as forest by the Settlement Oﬃ  cer under the 
said Act, the area and boundaries of which are speciﬁ ed in the 
below, as reserved Forest.

Sඋඐඍඌඝඔඍ
1.
Name of the District
:
The Nilgiris
2.
Name of the Taluk 
:
Gudalur
3.
Number and name of the 
Village
:
No.1, Cherumulli 
Village
4.
Survey number of the 
Forest block
:
15/5
5.
Name of the forest block
:
Cherumulli Forest 
Block-2
6.
Extent of the forest block
:
15.31.0 Hectare, 
(or) 37.83 Acres
BOUNDARIES.
North:- The boundary line Starts from the tri-junction 
point of Survey Numbers 15/1, 43 and 15/5 of  Cherumulli 
Village, the boundary generally runs towards southeast along 
the southern boundary of  Survey Number 43 and then runs 
towards east along the southern side of Survey Numbers 
42, 41 and 38 of Cherumulli Village and meets at the 
tri-junction point of Survey Numbers 16, 38 and 15/5 of 
Cherumulli Village. 
East and South:- Thence, the boundary runs towards 
southwest wards along the western and  northern side of 
Survey Number 16 of Cherumulli Village and meets at the 
tri-junction point of  Survey Numbers 16, 15/2 and 15/5 of 
Cherumulli Village. 
West:- Thence, the boundary generally runs northwards 
along the eastern boundary of  Survey Numbers 15/2 and 
15/1 of Cherumulli Village till it meets the starting point.

HIGHWAYS AND MINOR PORTS DEPARTMENT
ACQUISITION OF LANDS
[G.O. Ms. No. 14 , Highways and  Minor Ports (HQ2), 
2nd February 2022, ¬î 20, Hôõ, 
F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2053.]
No.II(2)/HWMP/111/2022.—The 
Government 
of 
Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed 
in schedule below and situated in the North Vellore  in the 
Taluk of Vellore in the District of Vellore are required for 
Highways purpose to wit for Construction of proposed Road 
Over Bridge  in lieu of existing Level Crossing No.128 at Railway 
km151/12-13 in between Vellore and Katpadi Railway stations at 
km 118/8 of Krishnagiri – Ranipet Road and it having already 
been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be 
awarded for the lands is to be paid by the Divisional Engineer 
(Highways) Project Division, Vellore -6 after considering the cause 
shown by the owner or other persons having interest on said land 
as the case may do hereby  publish the following notice under 
sub-section 1 of Section 15 of Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 
(Tamil Nadu Act 34/2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section 1 of Section 15 of Tamil Nadu 
Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34/2002) the Governor of 
Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the land speciﬁ ed in the schedule 
below measuring an extent of 5146.5 Square Meters of wet 
lands to the same, a little more or less needed for Highways 
to wit for Construction of proposed Road Over Bridge in lieu 
of existing Level Crossing No.128 at Railway km151/12-13 in 
between Vellore and Katpadi Railway stations at km 118/8 of 
Krishnagiri – Ranipet Road located in North Vellore, Vellore 
Taluk, Vellore District.
The Plan of lands is kept in the oﬃ  ce of District Revenue 
Oﬃ  cer, Vellore District and may be inspected at any time during 
oﬃ  ce hours.

[G.O. (D). No.19, Highways and Minor Ports (HW1),
1st February 2022, ¬î 19, Hôõ,
F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2053.]
No.II(2)/HWMP/112/2022.—The  Governor  of  Tamil  Nadu 
having been satisﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in the Schedule 
below are acquired for Highways purpose to wit for the 
extension of four lane to six lane Poonamallee - Avadi Road 
at No.49, Kattupakkam Village, Poonamallee Taluk
in Tiruvallur District and it having  already been decided
that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the 
lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by 
Chief Engineer (H), Construction and Maintenance  and after 
having considered  the cause shown by the owners or other 
persons having interest on such lands as the case may be, do 
hereby publish the following notice under sub-section (1) of 
Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu 
Act, 34 of 2002.)
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu 
Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands speciﬁ ed in the 
Schedule below and measuring to an extent of 08404 Square 
Meters for the purpose for extension of four lane to six lane 
Poonamallee - Avadi Road at No.49, Kattupakkam Village, 
Poonamallee Taluk in Tiruvallur District.
The  plan of the lands under acquisition are kept in the 
oﬃ  ce of the District Revenue Oﬃ  cer, Tiruvallur and oﬃ  ce of 
the Tahsildar, Poonamallee and may be inspected at any time 
during oﬃ  ce hours.

HOME DEPARTMENT
Constitution of a Sub Court at Thiruthuraipoondi in 
Tiruvarur District under the Tamil Nadu Civil Courts Act.
[G.O. Ms. No. 62,  Home (Court-III), 4th February 2022, 
¬î 22, Hôõ, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2053.]
No. II(2)/HO/113/2022.—In exercise of the powers 
conferred by the ﬁ rst paragraph of section 4 of the Tamil Nadu 
Civil Courts Act, 1873 (Central Act III  of 1873), the Governor of 
Tamil Nadu, hereby alters the number of Subordinate Judges 
to be appointed under the said Act for Tiruvarur District as 
THREE with eﬀ ect from the date on which the Subordinate 
Judge, assumes charge of the Subordinate Judge's Court at 
Thiruthuraipoondi.
NOTIFICATION-II
[G.O. Ms. No. 62,  Home (Court-III), 4th February 2022, 
¬î 22, Hôõ, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2053.]
No. II(2)/HO/114/2022.—In exercise of the powers 
conferred by the second paragraph of section 4 of the 
Tamil Nadu Civil Courts Act, 1873 (Central Act III of 1873), 
the Governor of Tamil Nadu, after consultation with the 
High Court, Madras hereby ﬁ xes the number of Subordinate 
Judges to be appointed for the Subordinate Judge's Court at 
Thiruthuraipoondi in Tiruvarur District as ONE with eﬀ ect from 
the date on which the Subordinate Judge, Thiruthuraipoondi 
assumes charge of that Court. 
NOTIFICATION-III
[G.O. Ms. No. 62,  Home (Court-III), 4th February 2022, ¬î 
22, Hôõ, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2053.]
No. II(2)/HO/115/2022.—In exercise of the powers 
conferred by section 5 of the Tamil Nadu Civil Courts 
Act, 1873 (Central Act III of 1873), the Governor of 
Tamil Nadu, hereby ﬁ xes Thiruthuraipoondi in Tiruvarur 
District as the place at which the Subordinate Judge’s 
Court, Thiruthuraipoondii shall be held.
NOTIFICATION-IV
[G.O. Ms. No. 62,  Home (Court-III), 4th February 2022, ¬î 
22, Hôõ, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2053.]
No. II(2)/HO/116/2022.—In exercise of the powers 
conferred by section 10 of the Tamil Nadu Civil Courts 
Act, 1873 (Central Act III of 1873), the Governor of 
Tamil Nadu, hereby directs that in the District of Tiruvarur, 
the Subordinate Judge’s Court at Mannargudi shall cease 
to have original jurisdiction over the District Munsif Court, 
Thiruthuraipoondi and hereby ﬁ xes the local limits of 
the District Munsif Court, Thiruthuraipoondi as the local 
Limits of jurisdiction of the Subordinate Judge’s Court at 
Thiruthuraipoondi with eﬀ ect from the date on which the 
Subordinate Judge, Thiruthuraipoondi assumes charge 
of that Court.
